	function geolocationtracker123(url){
	 //$('#body_loader').fadeIn();

        function initiate_geolocation()
	   {
            navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(handle_geolocation_query,handle_errors);
        }
        function handle_errors(error)
        {
            switch(error.code)
            {
                case error.PERMISSION_DENIED:
				faildtogetloc();
                break;
                case error.POSITION_UNAVAILABLE:
				//alert("could not detect current position");
				faildtogetloc();
                break;
                case error.TIMEOUT:
				faildtogetloc();
                break;
                default:
				faildtogetloc();
				//alert("unknown error");
                break;
            }
        }

		function initiate_watchlocation()
		{
			//if (watchProcess == null) {
				navigator.geolocation.watchPosition(handle_geolocation_query, handle_errors);
			//}
		}

		function stop_watchlocation()
		{
			if (watchProcess != null)
			{
				navigator.geolocation.clearWatch(watchProcess);
				watchProcess = null;
			}
		}

		/*function faildtogetloc()
		{
		  //alert("the user did not share geolocation data");

					});

		}*/

<script type="text/javascript">

	   $(function() {
    var cache = {},
        lastXhr;
    $( "#keywords" ).autocomplete({
        minLength: 1,
		 select: function( event, ui ) {
	  if(ui.item.flag==2 || ui.item.flag==9 || ui.item.flag==6 || ui.item.flag==5)
	  {
		window.location.href=ui.item.elem_id;
		return false;
	  }
	  $.ajax({
					type: "POST",
					data: { elem1: ui.item.label,elem2: ui.item.elem_id,elem3: ui.item.flag},
					url: "/users/busqueda_autocomp",
					success: function(msg){
						if(msg!='')
						{
							window.location.href=msg;
						}
					}
				});

      },
        source: function( request, response ) {
            var term = request.term;
            if ( term in cache ) {
                response( cache[ term ] );
                return;
            }

            lastXhr = $.getJSON( "/users/searchAjax", request, function( data, status, xhr ) {
                cache[ term ] = data; //TODO SEARCH  DATA
                if ( xhr === lastXhr ) {
                    response( data );
                }
            });
        }
    });
});

function mobile_sitesearch(e)
{
  if (e.keyCode == 13) {
	  document.getElementById('searchForm').submit;
    }

}

function callonfocus(){
   document.getElementById('keywords').style.outline='none';
   document.getElementById('closespan').style.display='block';
}

function cleartext(){
  document.getElementById('keywords').value='';
  document.getElementById('closespan').style.display='none';
}
</script>

{

function eventlink(elem)
{

	{ 
	 parent.window.location.href = elem;

	else
	{
	  document.getElementById('ctrlselected').value = 'no';

function triggerfilter_1(url)
	  {
		//alert(url);
		//var loc = window.location;
		
		var ordenpor=$('#ordenpor').val();
		var cat_name=$('#cat_name').val();
		var cat_id=$('#cat_id').val();
		var sub_cat_id=$('#sub_cat_id').val();
		var selected_region_id=$('#selected_region_id_1').val();
		
		if(selected_region_id!='' && ordenpor!='')
		{
			if(sub_cat_id=='')
			var orderurl	= '/eventos/region/'+selected_region_id+'/'+ordenpor;
			else
			var orderurl	= '/eventos/region/'+selected_region_id+'/'+ordenpor+'?cat='+sub_cat_id;
		}
		
		if(selected_region_id=='' && ordenpor!='' && cat_name=='')
		{
			if(sub_cat_id=='')
			var orderurl	= '/eventos/'+ordenpor;
			else
			var orderurl	= '/eventos/'+ordenpor+'?cat='+sub_cat_id;	
		}
		
		if(selected_region_id=='' && ordenpor!='' && cat_name!='')
		{
			
			
			if(sub_cat_id=='')
			var orderurl	= '/eventos/'+cat_name+'/'+ordenpor;
			else
			var orderurl	= '/eventos/'+cat_name+'/'+ordenpor+'?cat='+sub_cat_id;
		}
		
		//var finalurl = finalurl + "&filtro=mapa";
		window.location.href = orderurl;
	  }

function regioncheck(value,reg_name,reg_count)
	{
		if(value!='')
		$('#costo_'+value).attr('checked', true);
		else
		$('#costo_0').attr('checked', true);
		
		$('#selected_region_id').val(reg_count);
		$('#selected_region_name').val(reg_name);
		$('#selected_reg_txt').html(reg_name);
		$('#all_region_id').toggle();
		$('#region_link').removeClass("active");
		
	}
function show_all_region()
{
	var classname=$('#region_link').attr('class');
	if(classname=='')
	$('#region_link').addClass("active");
	else
	$('#region_link').removeClass("active");
	
	//$('#region_link').attr('class', 'Active');
	$('#all_region_id').toggle();
	var selected_region_name=$('#selected_region_name').val();
	$('#selected_reg_txt').html(selected_region_name);
	
}

function regioncheck_1(value,reg_name,reg_count)
	{
		if(value!='')
		$('#reg_'+value).attr('checked', true);
		else
		$('#reg_0').attr('checked', true);
		
		$('#selected_region_id_1').val(reg_count);
		$('#selected_region_name_1').val(reg_name);
		$('#selected_reg_txt_1').html(reg_name);
		$('#all_region_id_1').toggle();
		$('#region_link_1').removeClass("active");
		
	}
function show_all_region_1()
{
	var classname=$('#region_link_1').attr('class');
	if(classname=='')
	$('#region_link_1').addClass("active");
	else
	$('#region_link_1').removeClass("active");
	
	//$('#region_link').attr('class', 'Active');
	$('#all_region_id_1').toggle();
	var selected_region_name_1=$('#selected_region_name_1').val();
	$('#selected_reg_txt_1').html(selected_region_name_1);
	
}
function installorden(elem)
{
	if(elem != "")
	{
	  $('#ordenpor').val(elem);          
	  $('#fechas').removeClass("active");
	  $('#nuevos').removeClass("active");
	  $('#visitas').removeClass("active");
	  $('#' + elem).addClass("active");
	}
}
function set_subcat_count(subcatid)
		{
			//alert(subcatid);
			var event_subcat_count_ = $('#event_subcat_count_'+subcatid).html();
			//alert(event_subcat_count_);
			$('#event_subcat_count_indv_'+subcatid).html(event_subcat_count_);
			
		}

			$('.event_filter_all_cat').fadeOut();
			$('#scrollToHere').fadeOut();
			//$("#subcatfooter").fadeOut();
		}

	}

 <script type="text/javascript">
			function inscribime_footer(e) {
    var r = $("#subscription_email_footer").val(),
        t = $("#subsc_comp_name").val(),
        o = ($("#subscribe_check").attr("checked"), $("#subscribe_check").attr("checked") ? 1 : 0);
    $("#subscribe_error_footer").html(""), $("#subscribe_success_footer").html("");
    var s = new RegExp(/^(("[\w-\s]+")|([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*)|("[\w-\s]+")([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*))(@((?:[\w-]+\.)*\w[\w-]{0,66})\.([a-z]{2,6}(?:\.[a-z]{2})?)$)|(@\[?((25[0-5]\.|2[0-4][0-9]\.|1[0-9]{2}\.|[0-9]{1,2}\.))((25[0-5]|2[0-4][0-9]|1[0-9]{2}|[0-9]{1,2})\.){2}(25[0-5]|2[0-4][0-9]|1[0-9]{2}|[0-9]{1,2})\]?$)/i),
        i = s.test(r);
		
    return r ? i ? (document.getElementById("subscribe_success_footer").innerHTML = "<img  src='/images/arrow_loder.gif' alt='' />", void $.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        data: {
            elem1: r,
            elem2: e,
            elem3: o
        },
        url: "/companies/subscriptionfooter/",
        success: function(e) {
		
            var o = e.split("!@!@"),
                e = o[0];
            $("#subscribe_success_footer").html(""), "success" == e ? $("#subscribe_success_footer").html("<b>¡Por favor abre tu correo </b>(o carpeta de spam) <b>para confirmar tu inscripción!</b>") : "fail_1" == e ? $("#subscribe_error_footer").html(r + "  ya está inscrito" ) : "fail_2" == e && $("#subscribe_error_footer").html('Esta correo ya está suscrito a un máximo de 50 alertas de negocios, para agregar este negocio debes <a href="' + o[1] + '">cancelar tu suscripción a otros negocios</a>')
        }
    })) : ($("#subscribe_error_footer").html("El correo electrónico no es válido"), !1) : ($("#subscribe_error_footer").html("Por favor completa tu correo electrónico"), !1)
}
			</script> </div>

<script type="text/javascript">
function makestarcomment(elem,reference)
    {
                    var uid=0;
                if(uid==0)
        { 		
          location.href = '/users/mobile_login?ref=' + $('#paramurl').val();
          return false;
          //$('#scrollToHere').fadeOut('fast');
          //$('#mobileloginpop').fadeIn('fast');
        }
        else
        {
          $('#storevoteposted').val(elem);
          for(var i=1; i<=5; i++)
          {
            	if (reference=='details') {
		     var clas = "star1" + i;			
		    $('#' + clas).removeClass("select"); 
		}
		else{
			var clas = "star" + i;			
			$('#' + clas).removeClass("select"); 
		}		
          }
          for(var i=1; i<=elem; i++)
          {
            if (reference=='details') {
		    var clas = "star1" + i;			
		    $('#' + clas).addClass("select"); 
		}
		else{
		    var clas = "star" + i;			
		    $('#' + clas).addClass("select"); 
		}	
          }
        }
        
    }
    
    function locationhref(uniqueurl)
      {
	window.location.href="/eventos/"+uniqueurl+"/comentarios"
      }

    function limitText(limitNum)
    {
	// For pop page
	if(document.getElementById("UserComment").value.length>limitNum)	  
	{
	      document.getElementById("UserComment").value=document.getElementById("UserComment").value.substring(0,limitNum)
	}
	else
	{
	      document.getElementById("countdowndetails").innerHTML=parseInt(limitNum)-parseInt(document.getElementById("UserComment").value.length)
	}
	
	// For details page
	if(document.getElementById("UserComment1").value.length>limitNum)	  
	{
	      document.getElementById("UserComment1").value=document.getElementById("UserComment1").value.substring(0,limitNum)
	}
	else
	{
	      document.getElementById("countdowndetails1").innerHTML=parseInt(limitNum)-parseInt(document.getElementById("UserComment1").value.length)
	}
    }
    
   
function ireallylike11111(cineid,comment,rate,nodoublepost)
{
    nodoublepost = nodoublepost || '';
    $("#detailLoader").css("display","block");
    
    if(rate == '')
    rate='0';
    
    $.ajax({
    type: "POST",
    data: { elem1: cineid, elem2: comment, elem3: rate, elem4: nodoublepost},
    url: "/cine/votinglikestatus/",
    success: function(val){
    
    
    var voating_status = val.split('||||');	
    $("#detailLoader").css("display","none");
    if(voating_status[2]=='remove')
    {
    $("#goshow").css("display","block");	
    $("#megusta").removeClass("orngBtn fright disable_btn");
    $("#megusta").addClass("orngBtn fright");
    $("#goshow").removeClass("orngBtn fleft");
    $("#goshow").addClass("orngBtn fleft");
    }
    else if(voating_status[2]=='change')
    {
    $("#goshow").css("display","block");	
    $("#goshow").removeClass("orngBtn fleft disable_btn");
    $("#goshow").addClass("orngBtn fleft");
    $("#megusta").removeClass("orngBtn fright");
    $("#megusta").addClass("orngBtn fright disable_btn");
    }
    else if(voating_status[2]=='add')
    {
    $("#goshow").css("display","block");
    $("#megusta").removeClass("orngBtn fright");
    $("#megusta").addClass("orngBtn fright disable_btn");
    $("#goshow").removeClass("orngBtn fleft");
    $("#goshow").addClass("orngBtn fleft");
    
    }
    $("#gospan").html(voating_status[0]);
    $("#likespan").html(voating_status[1]);
    //document.getElementById('fancontentdiv').innerHTML = voating_status[3];
    //disablePopup();	
    
    }
    });
}

function ireallylike(cineid,comment,rate,nodoublepost)
  {
    nodoublepost=nodoublepost||'';
    $("#detailLoader").css("display","block");
    if(rate=='')
    rate='0';
    $.ajax({
      type:"POST",
      data:{elem1:cineid,elem2:comment,elem3:rate,elem4:nodoublepost},
      url:"/culturas/votinglikestatus/",
      success:function(val){
	var voating_status=val.split('||||');
	$("#detailLoader").css("display","none");
	if($.trim(voating_status[0]) == "failed")
	{
	  alert('Failed');
	  return false
	} else if(voating_status[2]=='remove')
	{
	  $("#goshow").css("display","block");
	  $("#megusta").removeClass("orngBtn fright disable_btn");
	  $("#megusta").addClass("orngBtn fright");
	  $("#goshow").removeClass("orngBtn fleft");
	  $("#goshow").addClass("orngBtn fleft")
	}
	else if(voating_status[2]=='change')
	{
	  $("#goshow").css("display","block");
	  $("#goshow").removeClass("orngBtn fleft disable_btn");
	  $("#goshow").addClass("orngBtn fleft");
	  $("#megusta").removeClass("orngBtn fright");
	  $("#megusta").addClass("orngBtn fright disable_btn")
	  }
	  else if(voating_status[2]=='add')
	  {
	    $("#goshow").css("display","block");
	    $("#megusta").removeClass("orngBtn fright");
	    $("#megusta").addClass("orngBtn fright disable_btn");
	    $("#goshow").removeClass("orngBtn fleft");
	    $("#goshow").addClass("orngBtn fleft")
	  }
	  $("#gospan").html(voating_status[0]);
	  $("#likespan").html(voating_status[1]);
	  if($("#fancontentdiv").length>0)
	  {
	   // document.getElementById('fancontentdiv').innerHTML=voating_status[3]
	  }
	  //disablePopup()
	  }})
  }

function megustapostComment(eventID,reference)
    {
        var uid = 0;
        if(uid==0)
    {
	location.href = '/users/mobile_login?ref=' + $('#paramurl').val();	
	return false
    }
    
     if(document.getElementById('storevoteposted').value!="" && document.getElementById("UserComment").value=="" && document.getElementById("UserComment1").value==""){
	    var ratevalue=document.getElementById('storevoteposted').value;
	    if(ratevalue=='1')
	    comment="(Mal)";
	    else if(ratevalue=='2')
	    comment="(Regular)";
	    else if(ratevalue=='3')
	    comment="(Bien)";
	    else if(ratevalue=='4')
	    comment="(Muy bien)";
	    else if(ratevalue=='5')
	    comment="(Excelente)";
	}
      else if(document.getElementById('storevoteposted').value!=""){
	  	if (reference=='details') {
		   var comment1=document.getElementById("UserComment1").value;
		}
		else{
		   var comment1=document.getElementById("UserComment").value;
		}
		
	    var comment = comment1.replace(/;/g," ");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/'/g," ");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/>/g," ");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/</g," ");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/&/g,"--^^--");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/#/g,"--^^^--");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/"/g," ");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/\?/g, "~~");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/\+/g, "--^^^^--");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/\//g, "--^^^^^--");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/\%/g, "--^^^^^^--");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/(\n)/g, "--^^^^^^^--");
	    var comment = comment.replace(/\:/g, "--^^^^^^^^--");
	}
     if(document.getElementById('storevoteposted').value=="")
	{
	    if (reference=='details') {
		    $('#starbox1').addClass("bordercomment");
		    return false;
		}
		else{
		    $('#starbox').addClass("bordercomment");
		    return false;
		}
	}
	
	if (reference=='details') {
	    $('#starbox1').removeClass("bordercomment");
	}
	else{
	    $('#starbox').removeClass("bordercomment");
	}
	
	if($.browser.msie)
	{
	    var browserInfo = 'ie';
	}
	else
	{
	    var browserInfo = 'notie';
	}
    
	if(eventID!="")
	{
	    if (reference=='details') {
		document.getElementById('loader1').style.display='block';
	    }
	    else{
		 document.getElementById('loader').style.display='block';
	    }
	 document.getElementById('megusta_button').style.display='none';
	 if(document.getElementById('storevoteposted').value !="")
	    {
		var ratevalue = document.getElementById('storevoteposted').value;
		$.ajax({
		type: "POST",
		data: { elem1: eventID, elem2: comment, elem3: uid, elem4: ratevalue, elem5: browserInfo},
		url:"/culturas/addUserCineComment/",
		success: function(msg)
		{					 
		if(msg)
		{
		var nodoublepost = true;
		//ireallylike(eventID,comment,ratevalue,nodoublepost);
		megustaeventireallylike(eventID,comment,ratevalue,nodoublepost,'');		
		if (reference=='details') {
		   document.getElementById('loader1').style.display='none';
		}
		else{
		    document.getElementById('loader').style.display='none';
		}								
		//document.getElementById('ajx_ratedetail').innerHTML = msg;
		//locationhref('');
		}
		}	
		});
	    }
	}

}


function megustaeventireallylike(cineid,comment,rate,nodoublepost,uniqueurl)
  {
    nodoublepost=nodoublepost||'';
    $("#detailLoader").css("display","block");
    if(rate=='')
    rate='0';
    $.ajax({
      type:"POST",
      data:{elem1:cineid,elem2:comment,elem3:rate,elem4:nodoublepost},
      url:"/culturas/votinglikestatus/",
      success:function(val){
	var voating_status=val.split('||||');
	$("#detailLoader").css("display","none");
	if($.trim(voating_status[0]) == "failed")
	{
	  alert('Failed');
	  return false
	} else if(voating_status[2]=='remove')
	{
	  locationhref(uniqueurl);
	}
	else if(voating_status[2]=='change')
	{
	  locationhref(uniqueurl);
	  }
	  else if(voating_status[2]=='add')
	  {
	    locationhref(uniqueurl);
	  }
	  
	  }})
  }
